> Before any action after compaction, reset, new session, or uncertainty, read in full: `web/rules/super-goal.md`; `tasks/TASKS/rules/create-prd.mdc`; requested `web/rules/generate-tasks.mdc`; populated `tasks/TASKS/rules/generate-tasks.mdc`; and `tasks/TASKS/rules/process-task-list.mdc`. Then read the canonical master PRD, canonical master task list (especially the first unchecked and every `NEW` task), and at least the latest three diary entries. Inspect `git status`, staged/unstaged diffs, and the active source initiative PRD/task list. Append a `post-compaction` or `resumed` entry and continue the exact recorded next action rather than restarting.

- **Leak proof:** In the exact test set, any populated miss-reason bucket identifies 6,484 non-goals with 0 goals. More severely, `shooterShiftAgeSeconds=0` identifies 1,022 goals among 1,042 rows (98.08%), while positive shift ages contain only 273/16,792 goals. The likely root causes are current-event miss outcome fields in the baseline preset and half-open shift lookup choosing the post-stoppage shift beginning exactly at a goal timestamp.
- **Remediation implemented:** Removed `missReasonBucket` and `isShortSideMiss` from every baseline preset and added them to the fail-closed forbidden feature set. Shift interval/stint lookup now prefers the interval ending at an event boundary, preserving the on-ice/pre-event shift rather than the post-stoppage shift. Added regressions for forbidden outcome fields, exact-boundary shooter age, and stint selection. Focused suite passes 32/32 and TypeScript passes.
- **Pagination discovery/remediation:** Freezing the trainer to 1,381 reference games initially failed with `UND_ERR_HEADERS_OVERFLOW` because all IDs were serialized into one PostgREST `.in()` request. Added live NEW 25.5/C0160 and changed explicit/reference selection to bounded 200-ID chunks with paginated range loops and deterministic global sorting.
- **Active verification:** A corrected reference-frozen rebuild/export is running under `/tmp/fhfh-xg-challenger-export-leakfree.*` with session `46177`. It must reconstruct exactly 118,299 rows, then rerun all global/state challengers with `--corrected-feature-contract`. No production model, predictions, registry, or lifecycle rows have changed.
- **Exact next action:** Let the corrected export finish, verify exact rows/splits and absence of forbidden features, rerun the three calibrated families/state partitions, quantify honest metrics and shift/miss leakage removal, then close 25.2/25.3/25.5 and determine the required production champion remediation checkpoint under 25.4.

- **Fantrax research:** Repository scope has only a placeholder and explicitly warns that official public API support was unconfirmed. This absence is evidence for caution, not proof that partner access is impossible.
- **Decision options:** **A (recommended):** implement owner-supplied Fantrax CSV/JSON import through the shared provider/league/team/preference model, with import-run status, validation, multiple-league/default-team UX, and no Fantrax credentials or scraping. Enables completion now with a stable user-controlled contract; does not provide automatic live sync. **B:** pursue official/partner access before implementation. Avoids unofficial integration risk but blocks NEW 25.2–25.4 and A-AUTH until access is granted or the owner approves an exception. **C:** build an unofficial authenticated-session adapter.
